34 /**
35   * inserts the CIResponsibleParty into the MDMetadata XML (where needed)
36   *
37   * @param xml
38   */
39 private class AddCIResponsiblePartyToMDMetadata(xml: Node) extends RewriteRule {
40   override def transform(n: Node): Seq[Node] = n match {
41     case e: Elem if (e.label == "contact" && e.prefix == "gmd")
42       || (e.label == "pointOfContact" && e.prefix == "gmd") => {
43       new Elem(e.prefix, e.label, e.attributes, e.scope, e.minimizeEmpty, (xml).toSeq: _*)
44     }
45     case x => x
46   }
47 }
48 
49 /**
50   * inserts the distributionInfo into the MDMetadata XML (where needed)
51   *
52   * @param xml
53   */
54 private class AddMDDistributionToMDMetadata(xml: Node) extends RewriteRule {
55   override def transform(n: Node): Seq[Node] = n match {
56     case e: Elem if (e.label == "distributionInfo" && e.prefix == "gmd") => {
57       new Elem(e.prefix, e.label, e.attributes, e.scope, e.minimizeEmpty, (xml).toSeq: _*)
58     }
59     case x => x
60   }
61 }

63 trait Xmlable {
64   /**
65     * creates JsValue from this class
66     *
67     * @return JsValue
68     */
69   def toXml(): Node
70 }
71 
72 trait Jsonable {
73   /**
74     * creates JsValue from this class
75     *
76     * @return JsValue
77     */
78   def toJson(): JsValue
79 }
80 
81 trait JsonableCompanion[A] extends ClassnameLogger {
82   val reads: Reads[A]
83   val writes: Writes[A]
84   val format: Format[A] = Format(reads, writes)
85 
86   /**
87     * parseOm2Measurements object from Json
88     *
89     * @param json
90     * @return Option if parsing error
91     */
92   def fromJson(json: JsValue): Option[A]
93 }

96   *

98   * @param title

109   * @param distribution
110   */
111 case class MdMetadata(fileIdentifier: String,
112                       title: String,
113                       abstrakt: String,
114                       keywords: List[String],
115                       smartCategory: List[String],
116                       topicCategoryCode: String,
117                       hierarchyLevelName: String,
118                       scale: String,
119                       extent: MdMetadataExtent,
120                       citation: MdMetadataCitation,
121                       lineageStatement: String,
122                       responsibleParty: MdMetadataResponsibleParty,
123                       distribution: MdMetadataDistribution
124                      ) extends Jsonable with Xmlable with ClassnameLogger {
125

127     val mdMetadataTemplate =
128       <gmd:MD_Metadata xmlns:gmd="http://www.isotc211.org/2005/gmd" xmlns:gco="http://www.isotc211.org/2005/gco"

242                 </gmd:geographicElement>
243               </gmd:EX_Extent>
244             </gmd:extent>
245           </gmd:MD_DataIdentification>
246         </gmd:identificationInfo>
247         <gmd:distributionInfo><!-- THIS IS FILLED BY TRANSFORMATOR FROM MdMetadataDistribution --></gmd:distributionInfo>
248         <gmd:dataQualityInfo>
249           <gmd:DQ_DataQuality>
250             <gmd:scope>
251               <gmd:DQ_Scope>
252                 <gmd:level><gmd:MD_ScopeCode codeListValue={this.hierarchyLevelName} codeList="http://asdd.ga.gov.au/asdd/profileinfo/gmxCodelists.xml#MD_ScopeCode">{this.hierarchyLevelName}</gmd:MD_ScopeCode></gmd:level>
253                 <gmd:levelDescription><gmd:MD_ScopeDescription><gmd:other><gco:CharacterString>{this.hierarchyLevelName}</gco:CharacterString></gmd:other></gmd:MD_ScopeDescription></gmd:levelDescription>
254               </gmd:DQ_Scope>
255             </gmd:scope>
256             <gmd:lineage><gmd:LI_Lineage><gmd:statement><gco:CharacterString>{this.lineageStatement}</gco:CharacterString></gmd:statement></gmd:LI_Lineage></gmd:lineage>
257           </gmd:DQ_DataQuality>
258         </gmd:dataQualityInfo>
259       </gmd:MD_Metadata>
260 
261     val rule = new RuleTransformer(new AddCIResponsiblePartyToMDMetadata(this.responsibleParty.toXml()),
262       new AddMDDistributionToMDMetadata(this.distribution.toXml()))
263     val finalXml = rule.transform(mdMetadataTemplate)
264     finalXml.asInstanceOf[Node]
265   }
266 
267   def toJson(): JsValue = {
268     Json.toJson(this)
269   }

272 object MdMetadata extends ClassnameLogger with JsonableCompanion[MdMetadata] {
273 
274   override implicit val reads: Reads[MdMetadata] = (
275     (JsPath \ "fileIdentifier").read[String](Reads.filterNot[String](ValidationError("String empty"))(_.trim().isEmpty))
276       or Reads.pure(UUID.randomUUID().toString)
277       and
278       (JsPath \ "title").read[String] and
279       (JsPath \ "abstrakt").read[String] and
280       (JsPath \ "keywords").read[List[String]] and
281       (JsPath \ "smartCategory").read[List[String]] and
282       (JsPath \ "topicCategoryCode").read[String] and
283       (JsPath \ "hierarchyLevelName").read[String] and
284       (JsPath \ "scale").read[String] and
285       (JsPath \ "extent").read[MdMetadataExtent] and
286       (JsPath \ "citation").read[MdMetadataCitation] and
287       (JsPath \ "lineageStatement").read[String] and
288       (JsPath \ "responsibleParty").read[MdMetadataResponsibleParty] and
289       (JsPath \ "distribution").read[MdMetadataDistribution]
290     ) (MdMetadata.apply _)
291 
292   override implicit val writes: Writes[MdMetadata] = (
293     (JsPath \ "fileIdentifier").write[String] and
294       (JsPath \ "title").write[String] and
295       (JsPath \ "abstrakt").write[String] and
296       (JsPath \ "keywords").write[List[String]] and
297       (JsPath \ "smartCategory").write[List[String]] and
298       (JsPath \ "topicCategoryCode").write[String] and
299       (JsPath \ "hierarchyLevelName").write[String] and
300       (JsPath \ "scale").write[String] and
301       (JsPath \ "extent").write[MdMetadataExtent] and
302       (JsPath \ "citation").write[MdMetadataCitation] and
303       (JsPath \ "lineageStatement").write[String] and
304       (JsPath \ "responsibleParty").write[MdMetadataResponsibleParty] and
305       (JsPath \ "distribution").write[MdMetadataDistribution]
306     ) (unlift(MdMetadata.unapply))
307 
308   def fromJson(json: JsValue): Option[MdMetadata] = {
309     Json.fromJson[MdMetadata](json) match {
310       case JsSuccess(r: MdMetadata, path: JsPath) => Some(r)
311       case e: JsError => {
312         val lines = e.errors.map { tupleAction =>
313           val jsPath = tupleAction._1
314           val valErrors = tupleAction._2.map(valErr => valErr.message).toList.mkString(" ; ")
315           jsPath.toJsonString + " >> " + valErrors
316         }
317 
318         logger.error(s"JsError info  ${lines.mkString(" | ")}")
319         None
320       }
321     }
322   }
